 - agar is aparaadh main pakade gaye to us aay yaa sampatti par jo kar banegaa uskaa teen guna jurmaana lagegaa
 - If you try to hide money by making another person a participant in it, you will be eligible to go to jail
 - sabko ek baar ke liye mauka diya jayega ki ve aisi sampatti kaa khulaasa karen or tees pratishat tex dekar chintaa mukt ho jaaen
 Apart from this, the government is also going to bring the benami transaction bill
 - ek lakh se adhik kii kharid par pan number anivaary kar diya gaya he
 But ASSOCHAM, an industry body, strongly objected to this bill
 asaucham kaa kahana he ki blike mani bill se sataane kaa or mauka mil jayega
 It has many drawbacks
 in kamiyon ko padhate hue laga ki koi dare yaa na dare ek varg ko is vidheyak se dar lag rahaa he
 According to Assocham
 
 
 - un logon ko suraksha mili jo ek baar main saare khulaase kar dena chaahate hai
 Those who do so are not punished under the Prevention of Money Laundering Act 2002
 - jo ek baar khulaasa kare usase tees pratishat tex na len, ye bahut zyada he
 - Taxes should be levied at the time of original investment or at the time of purchase and not at the current market rate
 - sazaa kaaphi sakht he, is sazaa ko inakam tex ke praavdhaan se joda janaa chahie
 This bill was to be introduced in the Lok Sabha today
 prakaash jaavdekar ne bayaan diya ki congress isse bhaag rahi he
 Congress leader Ambika Soni said that BJP had a problem when we wanted this bill, but when we are saying that there is widespread discussion, BJP is having problems
 vaise congress adhyaksh sonia gandhi ne buudhvaar ko loksabhaa main sawaal kiya tha ki ek saal se lokapal, kendriya soochna ayukta, kendriya satarkta ayukta kii niyukti kyon nahin ho rahi he
 Not only this, the financial powers of the Information Commissioner were handed over to the Government Secretary, whereas there is no such post in the RTI Act
 act ke anusaar kendriya soochna ayukta ke paas hi prashasnic or vittiya adhikaar the
 The government cannot control the work of the Information Commissioner in any way
 kendriya soochna ayukta ke saath das soochna ayukta bhi hote hai
 Sonia had asked that there is no Central Information Commissioner, in response to which Jitendra Singh first counted that there have been many times during the UPA when entire posts of Information Commissioners were not filled
 saath hi vittiya adhikaar soochna ayukta ke sachiv ko waapas saunp diye gaye hai
 Another important post is that of the head of the Enforcement Directorate
 agast 2014 se is pad par sthaayee niyukti nahi hui he
 There is also a case for amendment of the Whistle Blower Act of 2011
 raksha ko ab is act se baahar kiya ja rahaa he
 The comments samprabhutaa or akhandta ke naam par raksha or samvedansheel mantralayon ko bhrashtachar ujagar karne vaale bahaduron kii pahunch se baahar kiya ja rahaa he
 Activists have questioned whether the integrity of India was endangered due to the Bofors, Tatra trucks and the agustawestland scandal being exposed? ek saal main lokapal nahin, soochna ayukta nahin, pravartan nideshak nahin
 So should we assume that the government is serious about corruption by making black money and PAN number mandatory
 baari-baari se gambhirtha kii vyakhya karenge
 Now when it comes to Lokpal, the past tense of English grammar is remembered
 ve bhi kya din the
 Then there was talk of seeing everything in Black and White, r or Par time, but now these pictures are really getting black and white and are getting fed up
 lokapal jokapaal or janalokapal or phir in teenon par tirpal
 The people who had made the Lokpal a question of life and death, they have gone in search of their Jan Lokpal by calling him Jokpal
 2013 se or nai sarkaar banane ke teen maheene se dilli main lokayukta nahin he
 Instead 1031 has become a call center
 jahaan ek maheene main sava lakh phone kol aae hai jinamein se 6000 shikayaton ko gambhir bataaya gaya he
 When corruption can be fought with the existing powers of Anti Corruption Bureau, does the Lokayukta of Delhi have less powers than the Anti Corruption Bureau
 main iskaa gyani nahin hum magar yah sawaal man main aayaa to uthaa diya
 1031 can be more effective than Lokpal, so why not abandon the idea like Lokpal
 isi tarah lokapal ke samaantar kaale dhan ko lekar andolan hua
 There is so much relief in this case that the investigation is going on under the supervision of the Supreme Court, by 12 May the SIT has to submit the status report
 lakhanu se kamaal khan ne report bheji he ki lokayukta ne jin mantriyon, vidhayakon or afasaron ke bhrashtachar kii jaanch report sarkaar ko saunpi he un par sarkaar koi karrwai nahin kar rahi he
 The Lokayukta of UP went to meet the Governor today, seeing that the report of thousands of crores scam case could not be acted upon
 hai court main janhit yachika bhi daayar kii gai he
 At least the current government could have taken action on the scams of the opposition party
 lokayukta ne apni jaanch main paaya tha ki mayawati sarkaar ne smarakon ke banane main 1400 karod ke ghotaale hue jisamen unke kabina mantri nasimuddin siddiki or babu singh kushvaha samet 199 log shaamil the
 The Lokayukta had said to recover money from them, but nothing has happened beyond the FIR
 yahi nahin mayawati sarkaar ne 21 sarkari chini milen bech deen jiske bare main sieji ne kaha ki ek hazaar karod kaa nuksaan hua he
 Investigation report has also been given to the government but no action has been taken
 yah saaf nahin ho sakaa ki lokayukta ne maujuuda sarkaar ke kisi ghotaale kii jaanch kii he yaa nahin
 On June 30 this year, there was a report in the Hindu newspaper that after the Lokayukta report, the Election Commission had abolished the legislature of BJP MLA Bajrang Bahadur Singh and BSP MLA Umashankar Singh, these people took the government contract which they did not take was supposed
 isi tarah aae din aap sieji kii report kaa zikr sunate hai or bhul jate hai
 Now there is a problem with black money
 wo aa nahin rahaa he lekin wo ab jaye nahin yaa aata rahe iske liye sarkaar ek nayaa kanoon laa rahi he
 According to The Undisclosed Foreign Income and Assets (imposition of Tax) Bill,
 
 
 - agar tex department se videshon main jamaa aay or sampatti kaa byora nahin diya to 3 se 10 saal tak kii sazaa hogi
 - If caught in this crime, then that income or property will be fined three times the tax that will be made
 - kisi duusare vyakti ko isamen hissedaar banaakar paisa chhipaane kaa prayaas kiya to bhi jail jane ke paatr banenge
 - Everyone will be given a one-time opportunity to disclose such property and be free from worry by paying thirty percent tax
 - iske alaava sarkaar benami tranjaction bill bhi laane ja rahi he
 - PAN number has been made mandatory on purchases of more than one lakh
 lekin udyogon kii sanstha asocham ko is bill kii sakhti se etraz he
 Assocham says that black money bill will provide more opportunity to harass
 isamen bahut sari kamiyaan hai
 Reading these shortcomings, it was felt that a class is scared or not scared
 asocham ke mutabik
 
 
 - Provide protection to those who want to make all the disclosures at once
 - aisa karne waalon ko privansion of mani laundring act 2002 ke tahat sazaa na mili
 - Do not take thirty percent tax from what you disclose, this is too much
 - tex mul nivesh yaa kareed ke vakt kii keemat par lagaae jaaen na ki maujuuda bazaar dar ke aadhaar par
 - The punishment is very strict, this punishment should be linked to the provision of income tax
 is bill ko aaj loksabhaa main pesh hona tha
 Prakash Javadekar gave a statement that the Congress was running away from it
 congress netaa ambika soni ne kaha ki jab ham ye bill chaahate the tab bijepi ko samasya thi lekin jab ham ye kah rahe hai ki vyapak charchaa ho to bijepi ko samasya ho rahi he
 However, Congress President Sonia Gandhi had questioned in Lok Sabha on Wednesday why Lokpal, Central Information Commissioner, Central Vigilance Commissioner have not been appointed for a year
 itnaa hi nahin soochna ayukta ke vittiya adhikaron ko sarkari sachiv ke haath main de diya gaya jabaki artiai act main aisa koi pad hi nahin he
 According to the Act, the Central Information Commissioner had administrative and financial powers
 sarkaar kisi bhi tarah se soochna ayukta ke kaam ko niyantran main nahin le sakati he
 The Central Information Commissioner is accompanied by ten Information Commissioners
 sonia ne poocha tha ki kendriya soochna ayukta nahin he jiske jawaab main jitendra singh ne pehle ginaya ki upie ke dauraan kai baar aisa hua he jab soochna ayuktaon ke puure pad nahin bhare gaye
 Also, the financial powers have been handed back to the Secretary of the Information Commissioner
 ek or mahatvapurn pad he pravartan nideshaalay ke pramukh kaa
 There has been no permanent appointment to this post since August 2014
 ek maamla 2011 ke visal blor act main sanshodhan kaa bhi he

 tippaniyan In the name of sovereignty and integrity, defense and sensitive ministries are being made out of reach of the braves who exposed corruption
